wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for subject prefixed tags
subject:wikidata and subject:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because subject:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q154912 vs (missing) article redirects from en:Olav V of Norway to en:Olav V
Olav V - an affected OSM element that may be improved

Q2677 vs (missing) article redirects from en:Wilhelm II, German Emperor to en:Wilhelm II
